 According to a report by Grant Thornton, a government with a positive attitude towards reforms, recent policy announcements and regulatory changes have given Indian companies hope for an improvement in the economy
 grant tharnton kii timahi antarrashtriya kaarobaar report (ibiar) ek vaishvik surveykshan he jisamen 36 arthvyavasthaaon kii companiyon ke 2,580 adhikariyon ke vichaar liye gaye
 On behalf of India, 89 percent of the people surveyed expressed confidence in a stable government and hoped for an improvement in the economy
 yah surveykshan aktubar-disambar, 2015 ke dauraan kiya gaya
 In this, people were asked how hopeful they are about their economy during the next 12 months
 is suchi main bharat ke baad 88 pratishat ke saath ireland duusare or philippines 84 pratishat ke saath tisare sthaan par rahaa
 Grant Thornton's Quarterly International Business Report (IBR) is a global survey in which 2,580 executives from companies in 36 economies were considered
 bharat kii ore se survey main shaamil 89 pratishat logon ne sthir sarkaar ke prati bharosa jataayaa or unhone arthvyavastha main sudhaar kii ummid jataai
 The survey was conducted during october-december 2015
 isamen logon se poocha gaya ki ve agle 12 mahine ke dauraan apni arthvyavastha ko lekar kitne ashanvit hai
 Ireland was ranked second in the list with 88 percent followed by India and Philippines with 84 percent
 valsad ke parsi anjuman trust ne 2004 main unki dost dilbar valvi ko apni maa ke antim sanskaar ke liye dakhma (tower of silence) main pravesh karne se manaa kar diya, kyonki unhone ek hindu se shaadi kii thi
 "he was asked to sit at a place scheduled for Hindus, a kilometer away during his mother's funeral
 mujhase yah bardaasht nahin hua,'' gulrukh contractor gupta ne khud ek hindu se shaadi kii he
 This is where the battle of Gulrukh started, which recently ended with an interim order of the Supreme Court, according to which he and his sister Shiraj Contractor Patodia, who were married in the Hindu family, had their 83-year-old parents, Adi and Dinaj Contractor Upon his death, his funeral will be allowed to go to the Tower of Silence
 haalanki, ve jor dekar kahati hai ki yah akele unki ladaai nahin he
 "I am fighting for the rights of women of the entire community

 Kanhaiya Lal of BJP has won from Malpura in the assembly elections held in Rajasthan
 malpura vidhansabha seat par bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ke kanhaiyalaal choudhary or congress-areldi gathbandhan ke sanyukt pratyaashee ranvir pahalwaan ke bich muqabla bataaya ja rahaa tha
 The BJP holds the Malpura Assembly seat
 jabaki ek daur main congress kii yah paramparaagat seat rahi he
 The 'vyas family' of Rajasthan is dominating the seat of Malpura, but after delimitation the political equation changed such that the seat came out of the hands of the Vyas family and the politics of the Jat community came to dominate
 2013 ke nateezeybijapi ke kanhaiyalaal choudhary ko 76799 ko vot milicongress ke ramvilas choudhary ko 36578 ko vot mili2008 ke nattejeynirdaleey taur par ranvir pahalwaan ko 31365 ko vot milicongress ke dow
 Chandrabhan got 27552 votes
 2003 results JJ Ram of BJP got 45876 votes
 Surendra Vyas of Congress got 35046 votes
 Political history of Malpura Damodar Vyas won the election as a Congress candidate from Malpura seat in the first election of 1951 in Rajasthan
 
 iske baad 1957 main damodar vyas dobaaraa se nirvirodh vidhayak bane
 This was the first and last chance to win uncontested election from Malpura seat, but in the next election in 1962, Swatantra Party candidate Jaisingh defeated Damodar Vyas
 haalanki iske baad 1967 main hue chunaav main vyas ne jitkar vaapasi kii
 Damodar Vyas son Surendra Vyas, son of Damodar Vyas, was elected MLA from Malpura in the 1972 assembly elections
 haalanki 1977 main janata party ke narayan singh se wo haar gaye
 In 1980, Surendra Vyas of Congress benefited from the disintegration of the Janata Party and he again became an MLA
 haalanki 1985 main janata party ne dobaaraa vaapasi
 In 1990, Surendra Vyas won again from Congress
 iske baad 1993 ke chunaav main jitram choudhary vidhayak bane
 The Congress fielded Saroj Gurjar in 1998 to replace Surendra Vyas
 aise main naaraaz surendra vyas ne nirdaleey rup main utar jeet hasil kii
 The ethnic equation of Malpura is dominated by Jat, Gurjar and Dalit castes in the villages of Malpura
 dalit 50 hajaar, jat 42 hajaar, gurjar 30 hajaar, saini 20 hajaar, muslim 18 hajaar, rajput 15 hajaar, brahman 15, vaisya 10 hajaar iske alaava kareeb 35 hajaar anya samudaay kaa vot he
 Assembly Equation: Rajasthan Assembly has a total of 200 seats
 inamen 142 seat saamaanya, 33 seat anusuchit jati or 25 seat anusuchit janajati varg ke liye arakshit hai
 The Bharatiya Janata Party emerged as the single largest party in the 2013 assembly elections and won 163 seats
 jabaki congress 21 siton par simat gai thi
 Bahujan Samaj Party got 3 seats, National People's Party 4, National Unionist Zamindara Party got 2 seats
 jabaki 7 siton par nirdaleey ummidavaar jite the

 Let us know the main features of this bill
 
 
 1
 The government wants to change the rule that Indian citizenship was granted to an illegal migrant who had previously lived in India for 11 years, but the government is going to reduce this period from 11 years to six years through this amendment
 2
 The Citizenship Act, 1955 provided for citizenship to people of all religions, but the new bill only provides citizenship to those of Hindu, Buddhist, Sikh, Jain, Parsi and Christianity, whether in Afghanistan, Pakistan or Must have come from Bangladesh
 3
 Under this law only those people who are residing in India since December 31, 2014 will be eligible for Indian citizenship
